\pagebreak

\centerline{\textbf{Hartman-Skrekovski Algorithm Path $3$-List-Coloring}}
\hfill\\

\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=.15, every node/.style={circle, draw, minimum size=8.5mm, scale=.175}]
  \node [fill=white!35] (0) at (0cm, 0cm){};
  \node [fill=white!35] (1) at (10cm, 0cm){};
  \node [fill=black!35] (2) at (5cm, 5cm){};
  \node [fill=yellow!35] (3) at (5cm, 2cm){};
  \node [fill=yellow!35] (4) at (5cm, 4cm){};
  \node [fill=black!35] (5) at (5cm, 3cm){};
  \node [fill=blue!35] (6) at (4cm, 1cm){};
  \draw (0) -- (6);
  \draw (5) -- (3);
  \draw (1) -- (2);
  \draw (5) -- (1);
  \draw (2) -- (4);
  \draw (4) -- (5);
  \draw (1) -- (6);
  \draw (4) -- (1);
  \draw (1) -- (3);
  \draw (6) -- (5);
  \draw (0) -- (1);
  \draw (0) -- (2);
  \draw (0) -- (4);
  \draw (0) -- (5);
  \draw (3) -- (6);
\end{tikzpicture}
